Shenbao Third Edition

Foreign Important Telegrams

Professor Piccard's Report on High-Altitude Exploration 75

Havas, Brussels, Belgium, 22nd: The Belgian Scientific Research Foundation recently received Professor Piccard's preliminary report on his ascent into space. It first describes the preparations and then states, "The weather report for August 17 indicated that the weather was good, so it was decided to depart the next day. The inflation of the balloon proceeded as usual, and the departure was considered excellent. The weight of the balloon was made uniformly balanced by various methods, so it was necessary to drop sandbags later to accelerate the balloon's ascent. We then stretched out the wireless telephone mast and verified whether the ropes tying the basket were secure. When the balloon rose to a height of 1,500 meters, the exit of the cabin was closed. During the ascent, the air pressure in the cabin was always equal to the air pressure at a height of 2,000 meters. All the instruments for measuring cosmic radiation and the wireless telephone were used without damage. All the telegrams we sent were received, and the replies were also prompt. However, the measurement work was extremely difficult due to the freezing weather in the upper atmosphere. The temperature in the cabin dropped to freezing point or as low as minus fifteen degrees Celsius. From 10:00 am to 11:30 am, the balloon reached its maximum height. At that time, the air pressure was approximately equal to the pressure of 73 millibars of mercury in the barometer. Afterwards, when the balloon descended, the vent was tightly closed, and everything was normal, and the descent was considered good. The air pressure in the cabin gradually returned to the air pressure at an altitude of 4,000 meters. When it descended to 4,000 meters, the exits of the cabin were opened. When it landed, the suspended basket only rolled a few meters, and some instruments were broken as a result, but it was not a major problem." The scientific results of this ascent were also telegraphed to Brussels, but the telegram has not yet been opened.

Havas, Chiavenna, Italy, 22nd: Professor Piccard and his party arrived at Chiavenna, on the border between Italy and Switzerland, at 7:00 pm. Residents along the road from Lugano to Chiavenna hung flags and decorations to welcome them. To avoid the crowds, Professor Piccard left Lugano without stopping.

Austrian Parliament Approves the Treaty of Lausanne 76

Havas, Vienna, 22nd: After a fierce debate, the parliament approved the Treaty of Lausanne by a majority of 82 votes to 80. Six members of the Christian Social Party, the Land League, and the Kampfverbund (Nationalist political group) voted in favor, while members of the Social Democratic Party, the Greater German Party, and two members of the Kampfverbund voted against.

Opening Ceremony of the Japanese House of Peers 77

Electric Communication Agency, Tokyo, 23rd: The opening ceremony of the 63rd session of the Diet was held at the House of Peers today at 11:00 am in the presence of the Emperor. At 10:30 am, members of both houses lined up inside the main gate of the House of Peers. The presidents and vice-presidents of both houses, Prime Minister Saito and other state ministers, President Kuratomi of the Privy Council, and other advisors stood respectfully in front of the gate to await the Emperor's arrival. The Emperor left the palace at 10:00 am, rode in a ceremonial carriage, and went straight to the House of Peers. After arriving, he received Prime Minister Saito and other dignitaries in the reception hall. At this time, members of both houses went to the hall of the House of Peers. The House of Peers was on the right, and the House of Representatives was on the left. Foreign envoys sat in the gallery on the second floor. At 11:00 am, Prime Minister Saito led his cabinet members into the hall from the right. The members all stood up to wait for the opening of the door on the left. The Emperor, led by Minister Lin of the Imperial Household Department and Minister Ichi-ki, ascended to the throne amid the most respectful salute of the members. Prime Minister Saito took the Imperial Rescript from the hands of the secretary and advanced to the throne, presenting the rescript to the Emperor. The Emperor received and read it. After the reading, Speaker Tokugawa of the House of Peers again advanced to the throne, received the rescript, and withdrew. The Emperor returned to the palace at 11:15 am, and the opening ceremony was completed.

India's Non-Violent Resistance Movement 78

Reuters, London, 22nd: According to the weekly report on India's non-violent resistance movement, in the united provinces, All-India Congress volunteers are still engaged in obstructing trains and cutting telegraph lines. Political leaders who have completed their prison terms have resumed their activities in several places as before. Employees of the All-India Congress in Bombay City occasionally gather to demonstrate. Other parts of the Bombay province are very quiet. According to reports from various provincial governments, non-violent resistance movements are only occasionally found, are insignificant, and are silent and unheard of in many places.

Liquidation of the Kreuger Match Company 89

Reuters, Stockholm, 22nd - The liquidation committee of the Kreuger & Toll match company has decided that the continued operation of the Swedish Match Company is beneficial to creditors and shareholders and can be revived in the future. Therefore, it is proposed to maintain a share capital of 90 million kronor. All those with debt relationships can extend the current suspension of cash payment method for three months from August 30th. Currently, the only representative who has not agreed to sign the draft agreement with the liquidation committee is the representative of the American bank. The American bank is the creditor for 5% of the company's debt, and its representative requested time to consider the matter. The liquidation committee's reorganization plan advocates that the bank grant the company the necessary time to repay the debt, and during this time, principal and interest can be paid, but the payment of principal must depend on the company's annual profit. The company's balance sheet states that the company's current assets are not far from the company's debts. All foreign bonds of the company are calculated at today's market price, and the value of monopolies and intangible assets has not been calculated. The liquidation committee believes that the maintenance of a share capital of 90 million kronor is necessary, but it should not be regarded as the committee's opinion on the value of the company's stock. The company will reorganize a special committee to study the possibility of separating the company's industrial and financial businesses. The liquidation committee stated that the company's profits will be used to repay the company's debts and reorganize its business within a few years.

Two American Women Set Endurance Flight Record 91

Reuters, New York, 22nd - The two women who flew into the sky a few days ago have now safely landed after setting a new endurance flight record. The two women, one Mrs. Marcellus and the other Mrs. Hutton, stayed in the air for a total of 196 hours, exceeding the previous women's endurance flight record by 73 hours. This flight is particularly amazing because Mrs. Marcellus felt unwell during the flight. Because Mrs. Marcellus suddenly felt pain in her waist after taking off, she used the radio to ask the doctor on the ground, who diagnosed appendicitis and asked Mrs. Marcellus to descend as soon as possible for treatment. However, Mrs. Marcellus refused, so during the days of flight, Mrs. Hutton had to take care of Mrs. Marcellus on the one hand, and drive the plane on the other. The plane, named "Flying Women's Boudoir," is now indeed used as a women's boudoir.

Swedish Match Company to be Reorganized 93

Preliminary Agreement Signed by Creditor Representatives

Havas, Stockholm - Regarding the reorganization of the Swedish Match Company, a preliminary agreement has been reached after discussions between company officials, domestic and foreign creditor bank representatives, and representatives of the shareholders' protection committees of various countries. The agreement has been signed by the aforementioned related representatives, except for the representative of the American Bank, who hopes to have an additional period to study the issue. The American Bank represents 5% of the company's interests. The Reconstruction Committee believes that it is most beneficial for all creditors and company shareholders to keep the match company active. The committee believes that the company will definitely get out of the current predicament in the future. Representatives of various banks requested that the Match Company be given a necessary payment period, during which the company may pay interest and repay a portion of the principal according to its annual profits. The committee proposed reducing the company's share capital from 360 million crowns (Swedish currency) to 90 million crowns. After the company is reorganized, all profits will be used to repay debts and consolidate the company's position. The above agreement includes an outline of the company's industrial restructuring and a large-scale downsizing plan.

Two Factions in Japan on the Manchurian Issue: Pro-War and Pro-Peace 95

Both Factions' Arguments are Very Firm

It is Not Yet Determined Who Will Win

Our Country Should Pay Close Attention to This

The Tokyo Yorozu Choho discusses Manchuria, saying: "Today, there is a major crisis hidden in the internal relations of Japan's financial world. Under the current economic structure, can we barely maintain the status quo? This is doubtful. Furthermore, from the perspective of external relations, it is even more worrying. What is worrying is that the global economy and the Manchurian issue, due to their impact, have greatly affected the domestic economy. Even if Japan's financial circles temporarily devise remedial measures, the outcome of the Manchurian issue will ultimately be considered a risk of setbacks and destruction. In this impoverished Japanese capitalist economy, only Manchuria can open up various difficulties, such as the supply of raw materials, the demand for products, and the migration of surplus population, all of which are Japan's path to survival. However, the Manchurian issue is not solely a relationship between Japan and Manchuria, but a problem involving China, the United States, Russia, and the League of Nations. It has the nature of a major international issue, and the difficulties of its complex problems cannot be fully explained in one sentence. In particular, it is difficult to predict how the current League of Nations investigation team will report to the League of Nations, and it is also unclear how the League of Nations Council will handle the investigation committee's report. However, based on Japan's current attitude towards China, Russia, the United States, and the League of Nations, the results may be unfavorable to Japan. At this time, our government and the public must have a major awareness. If the League of Nations Council makes a judgment unfavorable to Japan, what new situation will arise is a major issue for the future. The current poor state of the world economy is due to the harm of the World War. This is generally recognized by people from all countries, and the current powers, including Britain, the United States, Italy, and France, are all in a state of poverty. It is probably not a good thing to talk about starting a war. Here, current facts and past experiences have the labor of mutual restraint. However, it is difficult to assert that there will absolutely be no war. If the League of Nations Council opposes the resolution, can Japan, by starting a war with the United States and Russia, contend with the world in this international reform situation, based on Japan's position? Therefore, Manchuria and Japan, regarding how the new country is formed, is still a byproduct, and the disaster of war has already been conceived. If a war breaks out, what is the current level of our national economy? This is a major key to survival. Recently, public opinion in Japan has been divided into two types: (1) Recognize Manchukuo, fight to the death with the League of Nations, and if it is not as desired, do not hesitate to fight. This war must be united by the whole country, and temporarily try to maintain the current economic situation. (2) The current domestic economic conditions cannot withstand the pressure of foreign wars. We should avoid war, be willing to regard Manchuria as Chinese territory, and belong to Chinese suzerainty. This can ease the atmosphere of the League of Nations and gradually transform the structure of the national economy, so that it can withstand international wars in the future. The above two factions, regardless of the government and the public, stand against each other. In the future, it should be determined according to the direction of national sentiment. If the people tend to favor pro-war arguments, the government will advocate a tough stance. However, whether advocating war can achieve the goal of maintaining the economy is questionable. It is difficult for the whole country to unite to resist foreign enemies, and internal reform is a prerequisite. Regarding this point, I hope the people will pay close attention to it."

Central Committee Members Leave Lushan to Return to Nanjing and Wuhan 97

He Yingqin Returns to Nanchang to Command Military Affairs

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Lin and Central Committee members Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Weijing, Yu Youren, Wu Zhihui, Zhu Peide, He Yingqin, Chen Bijun, etc., gathered at Chiang's residence in Lushan several times to discuss and exchange opinions. As a result, Wang's resignation as President of the Executive Yuan was retained, but it is still unknown whether Wang is willing to withdraw his resignation. After Zhang Xueliang resigned as Director of the Pacification Headquarters, regarding the issue of military jurisdiction in the Northeast, it was unanimously agreed that at this time of strong neighbors pressing the border, it is not appropriate to make changes, and everything should remain as it was. The resignations of the various ministers were also unanimously retained to jointly overcome the crisis. In addition, regarding party affairs, it was decided to convene a plenary meeting in the near future to resolve all major current issues and decide on future policies. Regarding diplomacy, steps to be taken towards Russia and Japan and proposals for the League of Nations General Assembly were planned. Regarding military affairs, Chairman Chiang and Minister He gave detailed reports on the suppression of bandits. Comprehensive plans were also made for military resistance in Rehe and Yuguan in the future, the support of righteous armies outside the Guan, and the reorganization and distribution of troops after inspection. Most of the Central Committee members believe that during this difficult period, only unity and consolidation of the central government can save the country from danger. Now that the Central Committee members believe that everything is progressing smoothly, they only need to return to Nanjing to submit to the central government for approval and implementation, and the central government's relationship is important and cannot be without someone in charge for a day. Therefore, it was decided that on the 21st, they would return to Nanjing, Wuhan, Jiangxi, and Shanghai respectively. Central Committee member He Yingqin returned to the province to command military affairs due to the urgent matter of suppressing bandits. Today, after hearing the news that He and Xiong (Shihui) returned to the province from Lushan, people from all walks of life flocked across the river to Niuhang Station to welcome them. At 12:45 noon, He arrived with a radiant smile, nodded to the welcomers as a courtesy, and then walked off the train, heading straight to the headquarters to discuss bandit suppression plans with Chief of Staff He. According to those who accompanied He to the province, all the Central Committee members decided to leave Lushan today, with Chiang still returning to Wuhan and Wang and others returning to Nanjing. This meeting has new policies for suppressing the Reds and resisting Japan. The Red bandits Zhu, Mao, and Peng in southern Jiangxi have now suddenly left their lairs and are attacking north with all their strength. Commander-in-Chief He, in addition to secretly ordering the garrison to cut off their retreat from the bandit lair, also transferred large forces from Jiangsu and Anhui to Jiangxi. He will arrive in the province today or tomorrow. (August 22nd)

Progress of Bandit Suppression in the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui 99

The Bandit Nest of Xinji Will Be Resolved Under Siege

Implement the Joint Responsibility System and Execute Retreating Officers

Hankou Correspondence: The military situation of bandit suppression in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has taken a sharp turn for the better since the recovery of Qiliping in Huang'an. According to an official of a high-ranking military agency interviewed by the reporter, the two Red bandit forces of Xu Xiangqian and Ji Xun, entrenched in the border area of the three provinces of Hubei, Henan, and Anhui, have been cut off from all supplies since the National Army implemented a strict blockade. Their medical supplies, which were already extremely scarce, have become even more difficult to obtain. The wounded or infected bandits are almost waiting to die. In the battles of Huang'an and Qiliping, they resisted stubbornly and tried to fight desperately, but they were met head-on by the National Army, suffering heavy losses. Recently, the people in the bandit areas have felt grateful for the generous treatment of the National Army and have become aware, no longer being anesthetized by the Red bandits. Therefore, the internal forces of the Red bandits have gradually split. The National Army, seizing the opportunity, has advanced simultaneously from all directions in eastern Hubei, southern Henan, and western Anhui. Telegrams of victory have been pouring in in recent days. What can be recorded is: In western Anhui, the National Army front in that area stretches from Shuangqiu, Lu'an, and Huoshan to the south, covering several hundred miles. The deployment of forces is extremely strong. The Red bandits have been wary of this for a long time. As soon as they heard that the National Army was advancing, their main force moved from the Jihe Che'an area to the Dingjiaji Huoxingmiao area southwest of Lu'an in an attempt to resist. The National Army, having learned of the location of the Red bandit main force, ordered each column to attack from Huoqiu and Lu'an in separate routes, all with Dingjiaji and other places as coordinated attack targets. On the 18th, the First Column of the Left Route Army launched a fierce attack on the bandits in front of them in the Xiahedian and Hekouji areas, occupying the line of Wuyangji Quanxingji and Dougangji. When the bandit units fled south, they suffered heavy casualties due to the attack of the National Army's advance team, and countless military supplies were seized. On the same day, the units of the Second Column advancing westward fought fiercely with tens of thousands of bandits near Balipeng. The bandit forces were unable to withstand the attack and retreated to Dingjiaji, relying on the terrain to resist stubbornly. After several assaults by the National Army, advancing one after another, Dingjiaji was occupied by the National Army on the morning of the 18th. The remnants of the bandits fled in disarray towards Xujiaji and Qingliang Temple. The National Army followed closely and pursued, and captured both places on the afternoon of the 19th, killing and capturing many. The remaining bandits scrambled to cross the Jihe River and scattered in all directions, and are still being pursued. Dushanzhen Chufuo'an, west of Huoshan, was originally the old nest of the pseudo-Fourth Army. Later, because the National Army's advance into eastern Hubei made the situation critical, they went all out to support it, and sent the remnants of the pseudo-73rd Division, which had been defeated by the National Army in the Wuyangji area, and a brigade of the pseudo-75th Division to fill the defense in the south. Now, each unit of the National Army in western Anhui has sent teams to encircle and attack in separate routes. On the 21st, they occupied the nearby Nanyue Temple, and after another attack, they will be able to destroy their nest. In southern Henan and eastern Hubei, Liu Zhi led the columns to converge and attack, and after recovering Huang'an and Qiliping, they advanced separately to attack Xinji, the location of the bandit nest. On the 18th, they encountered 15,000 bandits on the line of Cao'ao and Fujiafan, and after a fierce battle lasting a day and a night, most of them were defeated, and many were captured. The remnants fled back to their old nest and held on. The National Army in southern Henan has pursued to the south of Huwan, approaching Xinji. Zhonggushan, 20 miles from Xinji, was reportedly captured by the National Army on the 19th. The barrier of the bandit nest has been lost and is under the control of the National Army. It can be resolved in a few days. The bandits in the Shangcheng area have been surrounded by the National Army, and all the key points have been captured. Recovery is imminent. The bandits in Luotian and Wushan in eastern Hubei are not large in number. Recently, they have been under pressure from the National Army, and their morale has been shaken. They seem to be fleeing north, probably fearing that the National Army in Macheng will intercept their backs and that there will be no way to retreat. It is reported that after Commander-in-Chief Chiang came to Hankou to supervise the suppression, rewards and punishments were clearly defined. He ordered each army to implement the joint responsibility system. Those who were wounded but did not retreat and those who were captured but did not surrender were given special rewards and

蘇州 100

The Suzhou case of Li Shunmei being accused is opened for trial. Liu Yongtai from Yunnan, formerly the Zhejiang Provincial Governor during the Qing Dynasty, built the Suiyuan Garden on Jingde Road in Suzhou. Recently, he opened the Garden East Hotel, possessing immense wealth. His son, Liu Yuzhong, was seen with his mistress, Feng Dayuan, leaving the Da Guangming Theater in the North Bureau, by his legal wife, Li Shunmei. She confronted them and took them to the police station. Afterwards, Feng Dayuan immediately hired a lawyer and filed a lawsuit in the local court accusing Li Shunmei and her daughter of defamation and assault. Yesterday (the 23rd), the trial opened at 10:00 AM in the criminal court. The audience was very crowded, especially with women. Judge Yang Yigu questioned all the parties involved: Feng Dayuan, Li Shunmei, Liu Zizhong, and Sun Caiyun. He then ordered the case to be closed for investigation, as not all witnesses were present. The court date will be announced after the witnesses come. Li Shunmei was released on bail.

Wuxi is strictly investigating troublemaking vagrant soldiers. The County Government held its 31st District Chief Meeting on the morning of the 21st. Chairman County Magistrate Chen reported that, according to provincial orders, many former soldiers were left along the Jing-Hu (Nanjing-Shanghai) railway line after the 19th Route Army was transferred to Fujian. He ordered strict investigation and apprehension. After consultation with Battalion Commander Wang of the stationed Wuxi Military Police, it was decided that any vagrant soldiers or militiamen causing trouble would be immediately arrested and handed over to the military police for severe punishment. Subsequently, Police Chief Wang Gong stated that there were few former soldiers of the 19th Route Army discovered in the urban area, but in the rural areas further from the city, there were inevitably small groups causing trouble. He requested that all districts pay attention and immediately notify the bureau for assistance if any unexpected actions occur.

Local Correspondence 2 of Shen Bao Third Edition

Kunshan County Police Force captures bandits. Five miles away from Zhangpu Town, inside the Wusong River, there was a government salt boat anchored around 9:00 PM the night before. Alongside it was a customs patrol gunboat for protection. Suddenly, three bandit boats approached. Soldiers on the boat saw them, and deemed them suspicious, shouting for them to stop. The bandits immediately opened fire, and the soldiers returned fire. The remaining bandits went to the salt boat to rob it. When the two sides were exchanging fire, Wang Xu, the Chief of the Zhangpu Public Security Bureau, learned of the situation and immediately telegraphed the County Police Force. Captain Zhang received the report and immediately led a platoon of officers to suppress and capture the bandits. Four people were arrested on the spot: Chen Gangzi, Wang Fusheng (also known as Wang A’gen), Wang Xiaobao, and Ding Guangzhou, along with three bandit boats. The remaining bandits fled ashore. On the 22nd, the four bandits were handed over to the County Government for legal proceedings.

Zhenjiang Provincial Government thoroughly investigates the Zhang Zuochen case. Zhang Zuochen, the County Magistrate of Suqian, was previously accused by the County Party Committee and fellow villagers in Beijing to the Provincial Government for corruption, dereliction of duty, and negligence in preventing bandits. It is now heard that the Provincial Government has dispatched personnel to thoroughly investigate and handle the matter impartially.

Yangzhou Township Headman kidnapped and killed by bandits. Li Wenzao, the Township Headman of Yangjia Township in Shaobo, was previously kidnapped by bandits who sent a letter demanding 10,000 yuan for his ransom. Through the efforts of his neighbor, Shi Guilin, who negotiated a reduction according to the address provided by the bandits, and the preparation of a feast by Li's family to entertain them, the bandits insisted on the original amount and tied Shi up, hiding him in the cabin of the boat, separated from Li by only a plank. The next day, Li died. Shi managed to escape but has not yet dared to report to Li's family.

Gaoyou City's North Embankment collapses for more than twenty feet. The newly built Eastern Transport Embankment north of the Fulu Temple outside the North Gate of this county collapsed for more than twenty feet yesterday after a rainstorm due to impure soil quality and poor tamping work. The section chief in charge is currently working to repair it.

Nantong thoroughly investigates the accounts of the detention center. The account books of the Nantong County Court Detention Center for the previous year were submitted to the High Court for audit. Many suspicious points were discovered. President Lin has now ordered Chen Xianwen, the County Court President, to thoroughly investigate.

Dispute over the existence of Rural Police Bureaus in Rural Districts. Various sectors in Nantong believe that the rural public security bureaus have no real power and, due to the lack of a definite police fund, are disturbing the people instead of helping them. A proposal to abolish all rural public security bureaus was passed at the County Administrative Meeting. The County Government has submitted it to the province for approval. Currently, the police officers in the districts, whose interests are at stake, are expressing opposition and have also sent representatives to the province to petition.

Problems with the selection of the director of the relief center. Zhao Jianhua, the Director of the Nantong County Relief Center, was dismissed by the Civil Affairs Department and the County Government ordered the replacement of Xu Gengqi and Zong Weichuan but both firmly declined. Currently, the selection of the director is extremely difficult.

Investigation into the ruler ditch murder case. Wang Zijian, who used to run a butcher shop east of the Confucius Temple outside the West Gate of this city, delivered payment for pigs to Zhang Changyong's house in the ruler ditch on the fifth of this month and did not return overnight. The next day, his body was found hanging on a tree in Zhang's backyard. His wife reported to the county for an examination. On the morning of the 20th, the County Government dispatched the newly appointed First District Chief, Ma Shaozhou, along with Zhang, the coroner, to conduct the examination. According to Zhang, the deceased was beaten before his death, which caused him to commit suicide by hanging himself. However, he was not originally hanging on this tree but was moved there after being discovered. In the afternoon, the deceased's mother and sister, the Hang Wang family, brought Zhang Changyong and his son to the County Government to complain. The County Government then dispatched Li Cheng, the trial judge, to open a court for interrogation. As a result, Zhang and his son were detained, pending the arrival and interrogation of Zhang's neighbors, Liu Songling, etc., to clarify the situation. They also ordered the Hang Wang family to quickly prepare a coffin for Wang's body.

The third batch of prisoners in Xiaoshan to be released under the amnesty will be registered. Since receiving the High Court's order to issue the amnesty decree and the recidivism prevention regulations, the Xiaoshan County Court has been registering prisoners in this county who are eligible for amnesty and commutation and reporting to the High Court for verification. The first batch released seven people, the second batch twenty-one people, and now there are more than twenty people in the third batch, and those with unexpired sentences will have their sentences reduced and be released. Once the registration is complete, it will be reviewed.

Night boat robbed, resulting in a loss of a thousand gold. The Shaocheng-to-Xixing night boat from Xiaoyangfan Bridge in Xiaoshan was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with ten bandits on board around 7:00 PM on the 20th. They looted wildly, seizing twenty-seven silver dollars and four foreign letters, worth about fifty-two dollars, as well as white silk and satin, totaling over a thousand gold. They then encountered an approaching boat and the bandits boarded their original bandit boat and escaped.

Banditry rampant on the border of Shao and Xiao. In Tianle Township on the border of Shao and Xiao, bandits are gathering in groups, recently divided into several factions such as the God of Wealth Party and the Rifle Party. At night, secret sentries are densely deployed in the surrounding neighborhoods, creating a sense of insecurity. It is heard that the Gods of Wealth invited from Shimenkuang are all hiding in the mountains, and when the army goes to suppress them, they cannot be found. Even a dozen or so members of the local defense corps cannot get close.

The 7th Division and 19th Brigade of Hefei defeat the Kuang bandits. Since the military campaign to suppress the bandits in western Anhui began from the central, left, and right routes, recovering Liu'an and Huoqiu, it has pushed to the west bank of the Fen River. The first two steps of the work have been completed. However, due to excessive heat and the prevalence of epidemics, the attack was temporarily suspended. Now that autumn has arrived, the left-wing Liang Guanying unit has completed its deployment in the areas of Linshan, Congjiabu, and Qingshan and is about to launch the third step of the anti-Red campaign in conjunction with the other two routes. Unexpectedly, Kuang Xun, on the morning of the 17th, personally led the 75th Division of the 25th Army and three independent Red Guard Brigades to suddenly attack the 19th Brigade of the 7th Division in Guojiadian on the central route of the suppression army. The attack came fiercely. The brigade fought back bravely. At noon, the outcome was still undecided. The 19th Brigade then launched multiple bayonet charges with their broadswords, killing many bandits. By around 6:00 PM, the bandits were unable to withstand the attacks and collapsed. It is estimated that over a thousand bandits were killed in this battle, and more than six hundred rifles were captured. The Third Army Commander Wang Jun opened a victory celebration in Hefei and telegraphed the front lines to commend the officers and soldiers of the 19th Brigade.

Special News on Education

National Physical Education Implementation Plan (Peach). The First National Physical Education Conference was declared closed on August 21st in the auditorium of the Capital's Lizhi Society. The results of the diligent discussions by experts in national physical education and other fields were systematically organized and summarized into the [National Physical Education Implementation Plan]. This plan, at the very least, can represent the general consensus and efforts of our country's physical education circles regarding physical education at the present time. Thus, these few words are written to respectfully wish for the realization of the plan and to offer some discussion. The most brilliant aspect of this plan is the determination of the status of traditional Chinese martial arts in physical education, correcting the past errors of blindly copying foreign physical education methods. This opens up a bright new path for the future of physical education in our country, which is a most fortunate thing. In recent years, the enthusiastic advocacy of Mr. Zhang Zhijiang and others, who have personally demonstrated, has been very commendable. [The Commercialization of Physical Education] is a characteristic of physical education in modern civilized countries, especially in the United States. Our country's physical education has imitated Europe and the United States, and its past achievements have mostly emphasized competitive sports. Schools often give special treatment to athletes. The plan states regarding the assessment of physical education: [Assessing individual performance in sports meets is only enough to promote individual progress. It is a mistake to use it as a standard for judging the overall physical education of schools and the public. Using it as a tool to promote the popularization of physical education in schools and the public is like trying to catch fish by climbing a tree. On the contrary, physical education assessment, which examines the physical education achievements of schools or urban populations, can promote the progress of physical education for the majority of the public and is a very reliable means of assessing physical education in schools or cities.] Thus, replacing [the commercialization of physical education] with [the popularization of physical education] is indeed one of the valuable aspects of this plan. Attaching schools to actual workplaces is most appropriate. This is advocated by emerging education. The plan proposes utilizing physical education schools near physical education fields in various places, such as establishing a National Physical Education College at the Central Physical Education Field. The planning is very good. If it can be implemented effectively, it will surely be highly effective. Physical education teaching in schools at all levels has traditionally been divided into required and elective courses. Typical curriculum arrangements are no longer valued by emerging education. How effective has the implementation of physical education courses been in the past? Is there no need for improvement in the future? This is the most crucial question for physical education implementation. The plan and proposals have not researched this. In addition, the plan provides very detailed regulations regarding physical education goals and a very complete administrative organization. However, there seems to be room for further discussion.

News has been received that the Ministry of Education is actively promoting physical education. Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua, in order to revitalize the national spirit, has been actively promoting physical education. He has expressed his commitment to implementing the resolutions of this National Physical Education Conference regarding various important physical education matters and has personally instructed the responsible department to pay close attention to their implementation. It is also heard that he is actively working on organizing a physical education committee and establishing a physical education inspectorate.

The Editorial and Translation Office of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau moves; the General Affairs Office remains in the Ministry of Education. After the establishment of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, it was internally divided into the General Affairs Office and the Editorial and Translation Office. Due to financial difficulties, it was unable to build the bureau's premises according to the original plan, so it continued to operate in the Ministry of Education. Now, because the premises of the former Editorial and Translation Office of the Ministry of Education are insufficient, it has borrowed office space from the Municipal Government's First Residential Area Management Office on Shanxi Road. It is scheduled to move the Editorial and Translation Office into the office on September 1st. The General Affairs Office will remain at the original address in the Ministry of Education. The new location of the Editorial and Translation Office is behind the Overseas Chinese Reception Center. The location is spacious and the air is fresh, making it very suitable for the residence of the editorial and translation staff.

The Ministry of Education orders all colleges and universities to quickly report military training performance reports. Nanjing, 23rd. The Ministry of Education issued a circular to all colleges and universities, stating that since it is the end of the year, the Training Supervisory Department urgently needs to collect survey forms to assess military training performance. They are requested to promptly investigate and fill out the previously issued survey on military training performance for high schools and above, and send it directly to the Training Supervisory Department for review.

The Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau held a graduation ceremony for public schools yesterday. Nanjing, 23rd. The Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau held the graduation ceremony for the seventh graduating class of public schools at the Capital Grand Theater at 9:00 AM on the 23rd. The Ministry of Education sent Zhong Lingxiu to deliver a speech.

Conference after the Independence of Rural Normal Schools in Jiangsu Province. After suffering from floods and warfare, Jiangsu Province has reformed its middle school rural normal departments into rural normal schools this year, with independent establishments. However, since the independent establishments are just beginning, each school has a common need for research on finances, curriculum, and organization. Therefore, the principals of each rural normal school convened a meeting on the 21st at the Zhenjiang Normal School to conduct research. The records of the meeting were as follows: Attendees: Wang Yinmin (Luoshe Rural Normal School), Han Wen (Jieshou Rural Normal School), Huang Tongyi (Qixia Rural Normal School,代 Han Wenqing), Teng Songshi (Huangdu Rural Normal School), Tang Minsheng (Wujiang Rural Normal School), Gu Yaopu (Guanyun Rural Normal School, Chairman Tang Runsheng, Recorder Gu Yaopu). (1) Formalities as usual, (2) Reports, (3) Discussions. 1. Regarding how each school should modify its curriculum to meet actual needs, it was decided that: (1) The Education Department should be petitioned to convene rural normal school principals and hire rural education experts to form a rural normal school curriculum standards drafting committee to compile the rural normal school curriculum standards. (2) At the next meeting, each school will present the results of their curriculum research for discussion. (3) The trigonometry courses taught in each school are not practical and should be changed to practical elementary arithmetic or simple surveying. 2. Regarding how each school should open rural elementary schools near the school for senior students to increase practical teaching experience and promote the effectiveness of normal education, it was decided that: Mr. Teng Yangzhi should be designated to draft a report to be submitted to the Education Department for approval, and the education bureaus where each rural normal school is located should be instructed to assist in the implementation. 3. Regarding increasing the standard of treatment for four-year graduate students of rural normal schools, it was decided that: The Education Department should be petitioned to revise the original treatment standards. 4. Regarding how to clear the student meal expenses prepared by each school, it was decided that: (1) The Education Department should be petitioned to quickly issue the old debts. (2) Before the old debts are cleared, temporary refunds will be issued. 5. Regarding what to do when each school has no funds and cannot start school, it was decided that: The Education Department should be petitioned to issue at least one month's worth of cash before the start of school to maintain operations. 6. Regarding how each school's equipment is rudimentary and needs to be supplemented, and after independence, the budget remains the same and expenses have increased, so temporary expenses should be generously allocated, it was decided to pass it.

Wuben Girls' Middle School normal school graduates run Guangming Elementary School. When the affiliated elementary school of Wuben Girls' Middle School has held entrance examinations for new students, the number of applicants has often been unexpectedly crowded. It is heard that this year there are only three vacancies in the second grade of the elementary school, but more than seventy children are competing for them, which can be said to be difficult to study. It is now heard that the graduates of the first normal school department of the school, feeling that the teachers of the mother school's affiliated elementary school are unable to cope and that the number of students is full, will, with the intention of serving society and testing the spirit of new education, rent a house in Wansheng Bridge in the West Gate to establish Guangming Elementary School. It is planned that all teaching facilities will follow the example of Wuben. Recently, they have been engaged in internal organization and filing procedures, and it will soon be possible to announce the enrollment.

Expansion of the Shanghai University School of Commerce. The curriculum of the Shanghai Hujiang University School of Commerce in the downtown area strives to be practical. The last semester was quite successful. The number of male and female students totaled more than 252. In the fall, they will strive to expand further. In addition to the university undergraduate program, specialized courses, and general courses, they will also cooperate with the press to open a journalism course and cooperate with the China National Industries Association to establish an industrial management training class with the aim of cultivating journalism professionals and training industrial management personnel. Wang Yingbin of Shishi Xinbao will be the director of the journalism course, and Dr. Qian Chengxu of the China National Industries Association will serve as the director of the industrial management class, responsible for guidance. The new student examination is scheduled to be held at 2:00 PM on August 27th, and registration and payment of fees will be on September 1st to 3rd. Classes will begin on the 5th.

Jiangnan College to be established. The local Jiangnan College has been operating for two years since being approved by the Ministry of Education. The results have been quite good. Last month, it was submitted by the Municipal Education Bureau to the Ministry of Education, requesting approval for its establishment. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education ordered the Municipal Education Bureau to send personnel to inspect and verify the college when school starts in the fall. Recently, the school is planning to make improvements and request establishment.

Groundbreaking ceremony for new school buildings at Jian Guo. After the original school buildings of Shanghai Jian Guo Middle School in Zhabei were destroyed, temporary school buildings were established at Route Tenant de la Tour, Route Remy in the French Concession. Efforts were made to restore the school because all Chinese people in Zhabei after the war should bear the responsibility for revival, and silently observing the situation, Zhabei is undoubtedly a perfect and safe area for students to seek education. Therefore, new school buildings are still being built at Tiantong'an Road and Zhiyuan Road, and expansion is actively underway. It is learned that the construction project has been contracted by Huang Yuchang Construction Company and has obtained the Municipal Public Works Bureau's license number 2281 and has begun construction. The founder, Fu Dezheng, and acting Principal Yuan Yeyu led many students who remained at the school to the new school site for the groundbreaking ceremony and inspected the surrounding area of the school site in great detail.

Plan for Jiao Zhou Road Zheng Feng College after its establishment. Zheng Feng College on Jiao Zhou Road was founded by literary scholar Wang Xishen, from middle school to college, has been in place for four years. Recently, it received the Municipal Education Bureau's Shangzi No. 3158 order, forwarding the Ministry of Education's No. 6289 order (details omitted). In recent years, Chinese studies have been neglected. If this continues, there is a fear of a lack of teachers. Those presiding over the college have deep research and are enthusiastically donating funds to guide future generations in the study of Chinese studies. In order to promote this, the Ministry has specially approved its establishment, etc. After receiving the order, the college, in response to the Ministry's encouragement, greatly expanded this semester to create a base for training teachers. In addition to the original Department of Chinese Literature and the Special Chinese Studies Department, two new departments, the Department of Political Economy and the Department of Art, have been added. The appointed department heads and professors are all specialized experts with rich experience. Therefore, recently, many scholars and educators have been actively registering. Classes are scheduled to begin on September 12th.

New Developments at Da Zhong Middle School. Da Zhong Middle School has moved into new school buildings at 43 and 43A J. S. Fforde Road due to the expansion of classes and the addition of dormitories. Its founders, Wu Jingxiong, Dong Kang, Zhang Zhirang, Chen Jian'an, and Yu Baocheng, strive for excellence in their studies. This academic year, they have hired Jiang Meisheng, a former professor at China Public School and Fudan University, who holds a Master's degree in Chinese Language and Literature from Columbia University; Lin Yulin, a Columbia University Master's degree holder and professor at China Public School and Guanghua University; Zai Qingyi, director of the English Department at Jiaotong University; and Sun Zengqing, a Ph.D. from the University of Hai'ao and former director of the Mathematics Department at Soochow University and now a professor at Shanghai Hujiang University, to teach mathematics, and Zhang Hongmei, a professor at Wisconsin University and Datong University, to teach physics and chemistry. There will also be Westerners teaching conversation in each grade. Recently, the number of students applying for admission has been very enthusiastic.

Pan Chuji Goes to the United States to Study. Pan Chuji, who has a Bachelor's degree in Literature and a Master's degree in Law from Fudan University, is talented in handling affairs. When he was at school, he often led mass movements. After graduation, he served as the secretary of the Fudan Affiliated Middle School, the director of the Translation Department of the Anhui Education Department, and a teacher at Anhui University, Anhui First Girls' Middle School, and Anhui First Vocational School. He also co-founded Hangzhou Middle School with his friends. He is diligent in his studies. His books [China's Land Policy], [Legal System], and [Political Systems of Various Countries] are now to strive for further study. He left yesterday on the President Taft to study [Industrial Public Management] and [Municipal Administration] at the University of Michigan in the United States. In the future, he plans to go to France from the United States to study rural cooperation, visit group farms and state-owned enterprises in Russia, and then return to China. It is also heard that he is carrying 3,000 copies of English propaganda materials about the Manchurian Incident, planning to carry out large-scale publicity internationally.

Local News: Two Bitterly Suffering Children See the Light of Day; Cruel Parents Each Imprisoned for Three Years; Motherless Child Gets a New Lease on Life

Ningbo native Dong Renbao, who worked as a newspaper vendor and lived in the back building of Wanshouchang Coffin Shop at 170-172 Meibai Road, engaged in the tailoring business. He married Guangdong Xiangshan woman Chen, who was exceptionally fierce and overbearing. He feared his wife and obeyed her in everything. She discriminated against Genfu, his son from his previous marriage, depriving him of sufficient food and warm clothing. Not only did Dong not reprimand her, but he also aided and abetted her, eventually locking Genfu with iron chains in a pile of wooden planks in the attic of the coffin shop for nearly two years. Recently, Detective Lu Gendi and Ding Baohua of the Xinzha Police Station discovered this and arrested Dong and Chen. Although Genfu was able to see the light of day again, his legs had lost the ability to move and his appearance was extremely emaciated. According to a diagnosis by a doctor at Renji Hospital, he needs three months of care before it can be determined whether he will be permanently disabled. Therefore, the First Special District Court ordered that the child be sent to the Women and Children Relief Association for care, while Dong and the others are held for questioning. This was reported in detail in previous issues. Yesterday morning was the date for the continued hearing of this case, which has been completely transformed. The two detectives, Lu and Ding, still brought the defendants and Genfu to the Second Tribunal of the First Special Court to await trial. Genfu's long hair had been shaved off by the Relief Association, leaving him with a bare scalp. His face had also become fairer, and the tattered and filthy black single shirt and trousers he wore had been replaced with clean ones by the Relief Association. However, his legs were still as soft as cotton and he was unable to stand. The officers carried him into the courtroom and allowed him to curl up on the floor. Judge Wu Tingqi frowned and shook his head. After Judge Wu Tingqi took his seat, he saw the child's condition and frowned and shook his head again. He then ordered a bailiff to carry him to the forensic office for a detailed examination. He was carried back after a while. It was reported that the forensic examination determined that the ligaments in both legs had contracted due to prolonged confinement, resulting in the loss of mobility. Whether this will lead to permanent disability will only be determined after a hundred days of recuperation. In addition to the legs, the abdomen also had latent diseases due to chronic malnourishment. Although his head, face, and limbs appeared bloated, this was a temporary phenomenon of emptiness after prolonged confinement.

Attempting to Accuse the Son of Theft

Judge Wu then began questioning. First, the police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated that the defendant had previously claimed that his son had repeatedly stolen items from others, and had been repeatedly warned without improvement, and was unable to pay compensation. Therefore, he had to resort to locking him up with chains. However, according to repeated investigations by the police, the child had only stolen gloves from a car once and was taken to the police station. Because the owner did not want to pursue the matter, Dong Renbao was called to the police station to take him back. If his son had repeatedly stolen, why didn't he say anything at that time? This shows that he is now trying to shirk responsibility by fabricating excuses. When questioned, Genfu admitted to stealing once. The defendants, Dong Renbao and Dong Chen, still claimed that the child was dedicated to stealing and could not be controlled, so they locked him up. Dong Chen even argued, claiming that Genfu had stolen from a certain family on a certain day, either clothing or hats, and that his father had repeatedly compensated, even pawning items. She insisted they could no longer tolerate it, so they locked him up. However, there was no evidence to support this. The police requested severe punishment. Judge Wu severely reprimanded the defendants, saying that they had no familial affection and were extremely cruel. Such cruel methods would not be tolerated even if applied to animals, let alone between father and son. He repeatedly sighed and ordered the debate to begin. The police lawyer, Wang, then recounted all the tragic facts and circumstances of stepmothers abusing their stepchildren since ancient times, to prove the defendants Dong Renbao's and Chen's actions of abusing their son due to fear of his wife. He stated that in order to protect human rights and maintain humanity, they should be severely punished in accordance with Article 294 of the Criminal Code, to serve as a warning to others.

The Violent Woman Should Be Sanctioned

Because the defendant did not have a lawyer, the judge appointed Shen Xiaoxiang as his defense attorney. Lawyer Shen stated that this tragic case was purely orchestrated by Dong Chen, with complete evidence and established facts. Such a violent woman should be sanctioned by law and there is no justification for leniency. Therefore, he declared that he could not accept the defense for the woman's part. However, Dong Renbao helped abuse his son because he was forced by his wife's ferocity. Since Dong Chen was the culprit, Renbao was somewhat excusable, and he requested that he be treated with leniency. Judge Wu then pronounced the sentence: Dong Renbao and Dong Chen were both sentenced to three years of imprisonment for the crime of jointly using methods likely to cause injury to harm a person, and the chains and other items were confiscated. Dong Genfu was sent to the China Women and Children Relief Association to be cared for. Thus, this thirteen-year-old motherless child can be said to have escaped from the sea of suffering.

Strange Visitor at the Public Security Bureau Claims to Be a Communist Due to Poverty, Requests to See the Director for Relief

One afternoon, a strange visitor, around thirty years old and poorly dressed, arrived at the Municipal Public Security Bureau and requested to see the director to report confidential information. After being questioned by the information officer about his name, origin, and whether he had a business card, the strange visitor hesitated. Because he had no business card to present, he took out an old one, which read "Wu Jingnan" (whether this is his real name is unknown). The information officer considered him inappropriate and did not report him. The strange visitor left dejectedly. Unexpectedly, the strange visitor went to the Sixth District Headquarters and claimed to be a member of the Communist assassination squad, and had assassinated important figures. Because he repented and deeply knew that the Communists had lost all conscience, and he knew that his crimes were heinous, he came to surrender and report confidential information to atone for his past sins. After repeated questioning by Director Zhang, he remained steadfast. Because the case involved surrender, he was sent to the Third Section of the General Bureau for interrogation yesterday. Under interrogation by the section, the defendant confessed that he was poor and bored, and wanted to see the director for relief. He was unable to see him, so he had no choice but to give false information at the Sixth District Headquarters, otherwise he would not be able to be interrogated by the bureau. The interrogator found that the defendant had committed this despicable act due to poverty and sent him to the Third Section's Relief Division for relief.

French Novelist Traveling the World Arrives in Shanghai for a Short Stay

Three-Year Journey Creates a Masterpiece

According to the Da Mei Evening News, German novelist Schmidt, only twenty-five years old, arrived in Shanghai today (23rd) after traveling the world on foot. It is said that he plans to stay for a few days before heading east to Japan, then traveling to the United States and various countries in South America before returning. Schmidt started in May 1930 from Hamburg, passing through Scandinavia and other parts of Europe before going to North Africa, passing through Morocco, Tunisia, Tripoli, Egypt, and other places before arriving in Asia's Palestine. He then took the route through Syria, Mesopotamia, Persia, Arabia, India, Burma, Siam, and Hong Kong before arriving in Shanghai. To save travel expenses, he mostly traveled on foot. He carried a large book with him, asking famous people from all over the world to sign it as a souvenir. He also carried a camera to take pictures of famous places. He plans a three-year journey, and after returning, he will write a new book based on his travels.

Major Kidnapping Case in Chuansha Town, Baoshan: Nine Members of a Family of Ten Kidnapped, One Shot

In the Bojiazuizi area, about three miles south of Chuansha Town in Baoshan County, the family of the late Li Jisheng (nicknamed "Foreigner"), who had some savings, became the target of bandits. Yesterday morning (23rd) around three o'clock, more than thirty bandits suddenly arrived, each carrying rifles, Mauser pistols, wooden clubs, short knives, and other weapons. They broke through the gate with huge stones and entered the house, kidnapping Li's wife Yan and four daughters-in-law, one daughter, one granddaughter, and son Li Pengming, a total of nine people. They also shot Li's younger brother Quanming, the bullet entering from his right waist. After the bandits kidnapped the people, they reorganized the team, called out names, and left. The injured Li Quanming was accompanied by someone to Shanghai on the Shanghai-Taicang long-distance bus at three o'clock in the afternoon. After arriving in Shanghai, the Shanghai-Taicang company arranged to send him to Baolong Hospital for treatment. At that time, the bullet had not yet been removed, and his injury was quite serious, and there was a risk to his life. It is also learned that Bojiazuizi is close to the Fotou Sea estuary. When the bandits entered the estuary, there were four fishermen rolling fish in the estuary. Fearing that their plan would be leaked, the bandits first took the four fishermen to the boat and swayed on the sea. After the nine members of the Li family were kidnapped, the four fishermen were released and they left leisurely. Later, the Chuansha Town Security Corps arrived after hearing the news, but the bandits were gone. The victim has filed a complaint with the Baoshan County Government requesting an investigation and arrest.

Mei Gengsheng Defrauds and Abuses His Niece, Sacrificing Her Life

After the Incident, Yinsheng Fled; Cohabitant Attempted to Extort Money

Ningbo native Mei Weiting, in his fifties, worked as a clerk in the Jiangdong Hotel on Xinkai River. Mei had a younger sister, currently twenty-seven years old, who was still unmarried. There was a fellow townsman named Mei Yinsheng, thirty-six years old, who ran a hardware store called Yiji Shenzhuang at No. 6 Cuihua Lane, Fuyou Road, Nanshi. His wife, Zhang, was the same age as Mei and had three daughters: the eldest, Meiyun, was sixteen years old; the second, Guiyun, was thirteen years old; and the youngest, Zhaoyun, was nine years old. Yinsheng and Zanting's sister developed a love affair from acquaintance and then a physical relationship from love. At that time, Yinsheng coaxed Mei's sister, saying that he had not yet married. Mei's sister thought she had someone to spend the rest of her life with and was overjoyed. Fearing that the family would block them after discovering the affair, they agreed to elope and lived together with Yinsheng at No. 8 Shunxin Lane, Laoshenfu Road, French Concession, living like a couple. However, good things are often difficult. This matter was discovered by Yinsheng's wife, Zhang, who was uncontrollably jealous. On the 19th of this month, she gathered many women to form a "women's army," marching mightily to the house at No. 8 Shunxin Lane, Laoshenfu Road. They broke into the bedroom, destroyed all the objects in the room, and scolded Mei's sister. The neighbors persuaded them to stop. Afterwards, Mei's sister was ashamed and angry. Seeing that Yinsheng had fled and had no way to complain, she immediately informed her brother Mei Zanting and told him the truth, saying that she was confused at the time and eloped with Yinsheng without notifying her brother. Now she deeply regretted it, but since things had come to this, she had no face to live in the world anymore. Therefore, she asked her brother to come here for the last meeting. Mei Zanting had been searching everywhere for his missing sister. Now that he saw his sister here, but fallen into such a state, he felt both sad and happy, and deeply hated Yinsheng for defrauding and abusing his niece, which was inhuman. He persuaded his sister and promised to come again the next day and find a way to negotiate with Mei Yinsheng. After Zanting left, his sister thought she had followed the wrong person and was so depressed that she hanged herself in the room that night. The next day (20th) afternoon, Zanting came to his sister's place as agreed, but the door was tightly closed and no one responded to his knocking. Knowing something was wrong, he immediately gathered four neighbors to force the door open. He saw his sister hanging high in the room, her body cold as ice, and she had been dead for a long time. Yinsheng had already fled and disappeared. Zanting immediately reported to the police. On the 21st, the court sent personnel to the scene to examine the body and determined that the deceased had hanged herself before death. The body was handed over to her brother for coffin burial. Around 8 p.m. the night before, Zanting was in the hotel when Lu Danru from Wuxing, who lived in the same house as his sister, suddenly came with his fellow townsmen Lu Jingming, Jiang Jiying, and Guo Wenjie, claiming to have important matters to discuss at a certain place. Zanting did not suspect anything and rashly followed them. They arrived at Mei Yinsheng's house at No. 6 Huacui Lane and loudly said, "We are detectives from the police station and have come to arrest Yinsheng." At that time, the neighbors in the lane were alarmed and came out to watch. The beat officer Sun Yuwang saw the situation and came to inquire. Lu Jingming immediately showed his card, saying, "I am an adjutant from a certain place, and I am here to arrest an important criminal. After arresting him, I will send him to your office." Officer Sun immediately returned to the Second Station of the First District to report. Chief Bao ordered Officer Sun to rush back to monitor. Officer Sun rushed back to the original place, but seeing that Yinsheng was not in the village, he dragged the village staff Zhang Xingsheng and Zhang Kun towards the French Concession of Xinkai River. Officer Sun immediately quickened his pace and caught up. When he reached the intersection of Minguo Road, he called the beat officer from that place and intercepted everyone and brought them back to the station. During the preliminary interrogation by the chief of the station, Mei Zanting explained the situation. Lu Danru confessed that he was forty-two years old and that Mei Yinsheng had killed someone's daughter and now refused to show his face. He and the deceased lived in the same house, and he was really upset when he saw this incident. Therefore, he specially invited friends Lu Jingming and others to come to reason with Yinsheng. Lu Jingming confessed that he was twenty-seven years old and lived at No. 30 Duojia Road, Santai Wharf. Jiang Jiying confessed that he was twenty-nine years old, a local, and lived at No. 2, Lane 105, South District Street. Guo Wenjie confessed that he was thirty-eight years old, from Changzhou, and lived at No. 7 Deshun Lane, Chezhan Road. The other confessions were the same as Lu's. Zhang Xingsheng and Zhang Kun both claimed that Lu and others came to the village to arrest our boss but did not find him, so they dragged us out. As for everything else, they did not know. Since Mei Yinsheng had illicit relations with Mei Zanting's sister, it had nothing to do with Lu and others. Now that they went to Yinsheng's village to reason with Yinsheng, there was no need to drag his village staff to the French Concession. It was obvious that there was an attempt to extort money by framing someone. It should be reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for thorough investigation and strict punishment.

China National Aviation Corporation Ships Seventeen Crates of Cylinders from the United States

National Railway Freight Transportation Liability Regulations (3)

(3) If goods arrive at the destination station and are unclaimed for six months, and the shipper still has not provided instructions on how to handle them, or the consignee still refuses to accept them, the railway will auction off the goods or take other appropriate measures that the railway deems appropriate. Article 33: Auction of goods. If goods are auctioned off, after deducting transportation and miscellaneous expenses, if there is a surplus, the railway will hold it in custody for one year from the date of the auction. Within one year, the shipper or consignee may at any time provide a reliable guarantor, fill out a "Request for Surplus Payment," and after the railway verifies that the guarantor is qualified, collect the surplus. If it is not claimed after the deadline, it will become the property of the railway. If the proceeds from the sale are insufficient to cover all expenses, the shipper or consignee shall be responsible for making up the difference. However, when the railway decides to implement the auction, it should, to the extent possible, notify the shipper or consignee. (Chapter 5: Railway and Merchant Responsibilities) Article 34: Railway's Responsibility. For goods entrusted to the railway for transportation, except as otherwise provided in these regulations, the railway is fully responsible. However, the railway is not liable for compensation for losses that cannot be proven to be the fault of the railway. Article 35: Term of Railway's Responsibility. The term of the railway's responsibility for transported goods begins at the time of acceptance and ends when the goods are delivered to the consignee. However, if the goods arrive at the destination station and are not picked up after six business hours, storage fees and/or late fees will be charged according to regulations. For goods sent to or arriving at dedicated sidings, the term of the railway's responsibility begins when the freight car is introduced into the railway freight yard and the railway personnel verify the goods and issue a freight receipt, or a bill of lading. At the destination station, it ends when the freight car is sent to a suitable location in the dedicated siding and the consignee signs for receipt. Article 36: Losses for which the railway is not responsible. The railway is not responsible for the loss or damage of goods for any of the following reasons: (1) The loss or damage of goods is due to natural disasters, incidents, or other unforeseen events that cannot be resisted by human force. (2) If several types of easily damaged items are packed in the same package and cause damage to each other. (3) If easily damaged items are damaged or broken due to improper packaging. (4) If the seals of barrels, bottles, baskets, cans, etc. are not strong or firm, resulting in leakage or water vapor evaporation, fermentation, decay, and loss, damage, or reduction in value or weight of the goods. (5) If the quality and weight of the goods naturally shrink. (6) If the goods have combustible properties and spontaneously combust. (7) If easily perishable goods, such as fish, fresh meat, fresh fruit, vegetables, flowers, seedlings, ice, and dead poultry, etc., naturally decay. (8) If the original items of the goods are damp and cause mildew, light weight, or the goods are damaged by rats or insects. (9) If the loss of goods is due to the negligence or forgetfulness of the shipper, consignee, or accompanying caretaker. (10) If the goods are loaded and unloaded by the merchant himself, the goods are damaged due to improper loading or unloading. (11) If the goods are shipped without declaring the true situation and suffer losses. (12) If the goods are delayed in time due to various reasons and their market value is reduced. (13) If the goods are lost due to quarantine or epidemic prevention. (To be continued)

Second Special Court Destroys Narcotics and Gambling Equipment Yesterday

French Concession, Jiangsu, Shanghai

The Second Special District Court scheduled the third destruction of narcotics and narcotics-related items seized during the three months from April to the end of June, and gambling equipment seized during the five months from February to the end of June. Earlier, President Ying Shi and Chief Prosecutor Chen Beisan reported to the High Second Branch of the Ministry of Justice, and sent letters to various agencies in Shanghai, requesting that representatives be sent to the scene to monitor the situation. This was reported in previous issues. The day before yesterday, the General Affairs Section built a mat shed in the open space east of the court and cleared the debris in the area. Yesterday morning, the Director of the Accounting Section, Wei Yuzhang, supervised the staff to move the items from the Stolen Goods Section to the area, arranged them one by one, and set up seats, preparing firewood, kerosene, salt, and other ignition materials. Zhang Dachun, Secretary of the High Second Branch of the Ministry of Justice, arrived at the scene to monitor the destruction at 9 a.m. Representatives from other agencies who arrived included Jia Chen from the Municipal Government; Zheng Youshang from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters; Yang Renrong from the China National Anti-Drug Association; Ren Bin from the Municipal Party Headquarters; Zhang Zhuozai from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau; He Zeren from the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Wang Zongjian from the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office; Zhang Zhengxue from the Lawyers Association; Sun Zhiyu from the High Second Branch; Zhu Mingkang from the High Second Branch Prosecutor's Office; Tang Zaili from the High Third Branch; Lin Xichou from the High Second/Third Branch Prosecutor's Office; Fang Xun from the District Court; Ju Zhijing from the First Special Court; Qi Yu from the First Special Court Prosecutor's Office; and Deputy Chief Detective Bai Erde from the French Police Department. They were successively welcomed by President Ying, Chief Prosecutor Chen, and Chief Secretary Xiao Jinfang, and seated. Each representative was given a copy of the list of narcotics and gambling equipment. At 9:30 a.m., Secretary Xiao and Director Wei ordered the staff to move the narcotics piece by piece in front of the representatives to inspect the seals and weigh them, and then set them on fire, adding kerosene and salt. Flames shot up and the stench was pungent. The burning continued until 3 p.m. when the representatives left. A total of 730 narcotics cases were destroyed this time, including 1,450 opium pipes and red pill pipes, 1,655 lamps, 95 catties, 14 taels, and a half-pound of opium, 46 large and small packages and 12 pieces, 3麻袋麻袋 of opium dross, 48 catties of fake opium, 3 pieces of fake opium, 180 opium bubbles, 32 small packages, 4 taels of opium, 12 packages of opium, 853 boxes of opium, and 3 cans of opium, totaling approximately 400 to 500 catties. There were 6,067 red pills, 79 bags and 203 packages, 16 and a half pounds of red pill material, and 28 strips. There were also countless other opium pipes, opium pipes, pliers, copper spoons, opium pots, and morphine manufacturing equipment. Six cases, including Xu Chengxiang's, were temporarily suspended because the appeals were not finalized. In addition, there were 82 gambling cases, such as 397 flower lottery tickets, one roulette wheel, dice cups, dice, playing cards, mahjong tiles, etc., all of which were destroyed.

Ruan Yao, a Chinese detective of the Xinzha Police Station, and Sun Jishen, a Chinese detective, recently received information from an informant that Zheng Lihao, the owner of Xinghua Printing House at No. 29 Hele Lane, Xinzha Road, specialized in printing obscene "spring palace" pictures related to public morals and sold them in the market for profit. On the evening of yesterday, at 8:30 p.m., they secretly went to the address and arrested Zheng, seizing a book of obscene spring palace pictures and taking him back to the police station. The detectives went to arrest Zhu but were unsuccessful. They only seized 1,000 obscene pictures (each with four photos) and 20,000 similar photos from Zhu's house at No. 641 Shanhai Pass Road. They took them all to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Wu interrogated them. The police lawyer said that according to Article 251 of the Criminal Code, such photos are most harmful to young people in society and should be severely punished as a warning. Detective Ruan then reported on the situation of the case and presented the pictures for inspection. When questioned, the defendant's confession was vague. Judge Wu reviewed the confession and sentenced the defendant to a fine of 800 yuan. If he was unable to pay, he would be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The seized obscene pictures were confiscated.
